PROJECT(chromium-blink C CXX ASM)

CMAKE_MINIMUM_REQUIRED(VERSION 2.8.8)
SET(CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE Debug)
SET(CMAKE_POSITION_INDEPENDENT_CODE ON)

SET(PROJECT_NAME "Chromium - Blink")

# Verify the Toolchain file has been passed
IF(NOT CMAKE_TOOLCHAIN_FILE)
  MESSAGE(FATAL_ERROR "Please pass \"-DCMAKE_TOOLCHAIN_FILE=../Toolchain-<arch>.cmake\" when running cmake !")
ENDIF(NOT CMAKE_TOOLCHAIN_FILE)
MESSAGE(STATUS "Chosen Toolchain: ${CMAKE_TOOLCHAIN_FILE}")

# Location of Mojo source folders
SET(MOJO_SOURCE_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../mojo")

# Location of Base, V8 and URL source folders
SET(BASE_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../base")
SET(V8_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../v8")
SET(URL_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../url")

# Location of Skia source folders
SET(SKIA_SOURCE_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/skia")
SET(SKIA_EXT_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../skia")

# Location of Chromium-specific OpenGL headers
SET(CHROMIUM_GL_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/khronos")
SET(CHROMIUM_GLES2_EXT_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../gpu")

# Location of third-party dependencies
SET(QCMS_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/qcms")
SET(OTS_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/ots")
SET(WOFF2_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/woff2")
SET(BROTLI_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/brotli")
SET(ICCJPEG_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/iccjpeg")
SET(NPAPI_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/npapi")
SET(SQLITE_EXT_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/sqlite")
SET(JINJA_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/jinja2")
SET(INSPECTOR_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../third_party/inspector_protocol")
# OTS depends on WOFF2 which depends on Brotli

# Variable paths for required third-parties
SET(GRIT_DIR "${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/../../..")

# Verify a backend (X11/OZONE) has been chosen ; default to OZONE
IF(NOT BACKEND)
  MESSAGE(STATUS "Option \"-DBACKEND=<X11/OZONE>\" not passed; defaulting to OZONE...")
  SET(BACKEND "OZONE")
ENDIF(NOT BACKEND)
MESSAGE(STATUS "Chosen Backend: ${BACKEND}")

# CMake modules
INCLUDE(FindThreads)
INCLUDE(FindPkgConfig)
INCLUDE(GNUInstallDirs)

# Mandatory dependencies
FIND_PACKAGE(Threads)
PKG_CHECK_MODULES(icu REQUIRED icu-i18n>=52.0.0 icu-uc>=52.0.0)
PKG_CHECK_MODULES(harfbuzz REQUIRED harfbuzz>=0.9.22)
PKG_CHECK_MODULES(libwebp REQUIRED libwebp>=0.4.0 libwebpdemux>=0.4.0)
PKG_CHECK_MODULES(libpng12 REQUIRED libpng12)
PKG_CHECK_MODULES(libxml2 REQUIRED libxml-2.0)
PKG_CHECK_MODULES(libxslt REQUIRED libxslt)
PKG_CHECK_MODULES(sqlite REQUIRED sqlite3>=3.6.1)

FIND_PROGRAM(PYTHON_FOUND python)
IF(NOT PYTHON_FOUND)
  MESSAGE(FATAL_ERROR "\"python\" is required, please install it !")
ELSE()
  MESSAGE(STATUS "\"python\" found...")
ENDIF(NOT PYTHON_FOUND)

FIND_PROGRAM(GPERF_FOUND gperf)
IF(NOT GPERF_FOUND)
  MESSAGE(FATAL_ERROR "\"gperf\" is required, please install it !")
ELSE()
  MESSAGE(STATUS "\"gperf\" found...")
ENDIF(NOT GPERF_FOUND)

FIND_PROGRAM(BISON_FOUND bison)
IF(NOT BISON_FOUND)
  MESSAGE(FATAL_ERROR "\"bison\" is required, please install it !")
ELSE()
  MESSAGE(STATUS "\"bison\" found...")
ENDIF(NOT BISON_FOUND)

# Optional definitions
IF(BACKEND STREQUAL "OZONE")
  ADD_DEFINITIONS(-DUSE_OZONE)
ENDIF(BACKEND STREQUAL "OZONE")

IF(BACKEND STREQUAL "X11")
  ADD_DEFINITIONS(-DUSE_X11)
ENDIF(BACKEND STREQUAL "X11")

# Common definitions
ADD_DEFINITIONS(-DBLINK_IMPLEMENTATION=1 -DBLINK_COMMON_IMPLEMENTATION=1 -DBLINK_PLATFORM_IMPLEMENTATION=1 -DWTF_IMPLEMENTATION=1 -DINSIDE_BLINK -DCOMPONENT_BUILD -DUSE_AURA -DUSING_SYSTEM_ICU)
# Let us avoid errors with "PRIx*" macros within Blink code
ADD_DEFINITIONS(-D__STDC_FORMAT_MACROS)
# This is required by the third-party SQLite extension code
ADD_DEFINITIONS(-DSQLITE_ENABLE_FTS3 -DSQLITE_DISABLE_FTS3_UNICODE -DSQLITE_DISABLE_FTS4_DEFERRED -DSQLITE_ENABLE_ICU -DSQLITE_ENABLE_MEMORY_MANAGEMENT -DSQLITE_SECURE_DELETE -DSQLITE_SEPARATE_CACHE_POOLS -DTHREADSAFE -DSQLITE_MAX_WORKER_THREADS=0 -DSQLITE_MAX_MMAP_SIZE=268435456 -DSQLITE_MMAP_READ_ONLY=1 -DHAVE_USLEEP=1 -DUSE_PREAD=1 -Dfdatasync=fdatasync -Wno-int-to-pointer-cast -Wno-pointer-to-int-cast)

IF(CMAKE_COMPILER_IS_GNUCXX)
    ADD_DEFINITIONS(-std=c++11 -Wno-c++0x-compat)
ENDIF()


# PRE-GENERATION .TMPL -> .ZIP (bytecode)

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating .zip files from .tmpl...")

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p mojo/public/tools/bindings WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python ${MOJO_SOURCE_DIR}/public/tools/bindings/mojom_bindings_generator.py --use_bundled_pylibs precompile -o ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/mojo/public/tools/bindings WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})


# PRE-GENERATION .MOJOM -> -BLINK.CC,.H

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating -blink.cc,.h files from .mojom...")

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python ${MOJO_SOURCE_DIR}/public/tools/bindings/mojom_bindings_generator.py --use_bundled_pylibs --for_blink generate public/platform/site_engagement.mojom -d . -I../.. -o ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR} --bytecode_path ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/mojo/public/tools/bindings --for_blink --variant blink -g c++ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/..)
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python ${MOJO_SOURCE_DIR}/public/tools/bindings/mojom_bindings_generator.py --use_bundled_pylibs --for_blink generate public/platform/site_engagement.mojom -d . -I../.. -o ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR} --bytecode_path ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/mojo/public/tools/bindings --generate_non_variant_code -g c++ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/..)

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python ${MOJO_SOURCE_DIR}/public/tools/bindings/mojom_bindings_generator.py --use_bundled_pylibs --for_blink generate public/platform/modules/offscreencanvas/offscreen_canvas_surface.mojom -d . -I../.. -o ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR} --bytecode_path ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/mojo/public/tools/bindings --for_blink --variant blink -g c++ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/..)
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python ${MOJO_SOURCE_DIR}/public/tools/bindings/mojom_bindings_generator.py --use_bundled_pylibs --for_blink generate public/platform/modules/offscreencanvas/offscreen_canvas_surface.mojom -d . -I../.. -o ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR} --bytecode_path ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/mojo/public/tools/bindings --generate_non_variant_code -g c++ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/..)


# PRE-GENERATION .GRD -> .CC,.H,.PAK

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating .pak from .grd...")

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p blink/public/resources/ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND ${GRIT_DIR}/tools/grit/grit.py -i public/blink_image_resources.grd build -f ${GRIT_DIR}/tools/gritsettings/resource_ids -o ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/blink/public/resources --write-only-new=0 WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/..)

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/minimize_css.py ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/core/css/html.css --output_dir=${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR} WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND ${GRIT_DIR}/tools/grit/grit.py -i public/blink_resources.grd build -f ${GRIT_DIR}/tools/gritsettings/resource_ids -o ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/blink/public/resources --write-only-new=0 -E html_min_css=${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/html.css WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR}/..)

# PRE-GENERATION .IN,.GPERF -> .CC,.H

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p platform/ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p core/ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p modules/ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating .cc files...")

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_css_tokenizer_codepoints.py --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating .cc,.h files from .json5...")

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python core/html/parser/create-html-entity-table -o ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core/HTMLEntityTable.cpp core/html/parser/HTMLEntityNames.csv WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_css_property_names.py core/css/CSSProperties.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core --gperf gperf WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_css_property_metadata.py core/css/CSSProperties.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core --gperf gperf WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p core/fetch WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py platform/fonts/FontFamilyNames.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/platform WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py platform/network/HTTPNames.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/platform WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py core/css/MediaTypeNames.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py core/events/EventTargetFactory.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py core/events/EventTypeNames.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py core/html/forms/InputTypeNames.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py core/html/parser/HTMLTokenizerNames.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py platform/loader/fetch/FetchInitiatorTypeNames.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/platform/loader/fetch WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py modules/EventTargetModulesFactory.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/modules WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py modules/indexeddb/IndexedDBNames.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/modules WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_qualified_names.py core/html/parser/MathMLTagNames.in core/html/parser/MathMLAttributeNames.in --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_qualified_names.py core/svg/xlinkattrs.in --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_qualified_names.py core/xml/xmlnsattrs.in --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_qualified_names.py core/xml/xmlattrs.in --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_settings.py core/frame/Settings.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_element_factory.py core/html/HTMLTagNames.in core/html/HTMLAttributeNames.in --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_element_factory.py core/svg/SVGTagNames.in core/svg/SVGAttributeNames.in --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_css_value_keywords.py core/css/CSSValueKeywords.json5 core/css/SVGCSSValueKeywords.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core --gperf gperf WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_style_shorthands.py core/css/CSSProperties.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core --gperf gperf WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_style_builder.py core/css/CSSProperties.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python ${INSPECTOR_DIR}/CodeGenerator.py --jinja_dir ${JINJA_DIR}/.. --output_base ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core --config ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core/inspector/inspector_protocol_config.json --config_value imported.path=${V8_DIR}/src/inspector/js_protocol.json WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python core/inspector/CodeGeneratorInstrumentation.py core/inspector/InspectorInstrumentation.idl --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_element_lookup_trie.py core/html/HTMLTagNames.in --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_element_type_helpers.py core/html/HTMLTagNames.in --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_element_type_helpers.py core/svg/SVGTagNames.in --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_media_feature_names.py core/css/MediaFeatureNames.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_media_features.py core/css/MediaFeatureNames.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_runtime_features.py platform/RuntimeEnabledFeatures.in --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/platform WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating .cpp from .gperf...")

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND gperf --key-positions=* -D -s 2 platform/ColorData.gperf --output-file=${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/platform/ColorData.cpp WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating .cpp,.h from .y...")

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/rule_bison.py core/xml/XPathGrammar.y ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core ${BISON_FOUND} WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating EventFactory/Names.cpp,.h from .idl files...")

# Generate "EventInterfaces.in", then "EventFactory/Names.cpp/.h", from *.idl
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sh -c "find core/ -name *.idl | grep Event.idl > ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/event.lst" WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python bindings/scripts/generate_event_interfaces.py --event-idl-files-list ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/event.lst --event-interfaces-file ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core/EventInterfaces.json5 WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_event_factory.py ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core/EventInterfaces.json5 core/events/EventAliases.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core/EventInterfaces.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating EventModulesFactory/Names.cpp,.h from .idl files...")

# Generate "EventModulesInterfaces.in", then "EventModulesFactory/Names.cpp/.h", from *.idl
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sh -c "find modules/ -name *.idl | grep -E 'Event.idl|SpeechRecognitionError.idl' > ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/event_modules.lst" WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python bindings/scripts/generate_event_interfaces.py --event-idl-files-list ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/event_modules.lst --event-interfaces-file ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/modules/EventModulesInterfaces.json5 --suffix Modules WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_event_factory.py ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/modules/EventModulesInterfaces.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/modules WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_names.py ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/modules/EventModulesInterfaces.json5 --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/modules WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating ComputedStyleBase(Constants).cpp,.h from .json5 file...")

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python build/scripts/make_computed_style_base.py --gperf ${GPERF_FOUND} --output_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core core/css/CSSProperties.json5 WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating initPartialInterfacesInModules.cpp from .idl files...")

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python bindings/scripts/generate_init_partial_interfaces.py --idl-files-list core_with_deps.lst --gyp-format-list --output ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/modules/initPartialInterfacesInModules.cpp WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

MESSAGE(STATUS "Generating .cpp,.h V8 bindings from .idl...")

# We create lists for all "core" and "modules" .idl files
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sh -c "find core/ -name *.idl > ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core.lst" WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sh -c "find modules/ -name *.idl > ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/modules.lst" WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

# We need to remove one "core" .idl which doesn't work
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,core/inspector/InspectorInstrumentation.idl,,g core.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
# We need to remove some "modules" .idl which don't work
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/BluetoothRemoteGATTDescriptor.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/BluetoothRemoteGATTCharacteristic.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/BluetoothRemoteGATTService.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/BluetoothRemoteGATTServer.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/BluetoothDevice.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/Bluetooth.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/BluetoothCharacteristicProperties.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/BluetoothScanFilterInit.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/BluetoothUUID.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/RequestDeviceOptions.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/bluetooth/NavigatorBluetooth.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/imagecapture/MediaSettingsRange.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/push_messaging/PushSubscriptionOptions.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/VRFrameData.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/VRStageParameters.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/VRDisplay.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/VRDisplayCapabilities.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/VRDisplayEvent.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/VRDisplayEventInit.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/VREyeParameters.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/VRFieldOfView.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/VRLayer.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/VRPose.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sed -i s,modules/vr/NavigatorVR.idl,,g modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})

# Remove the now empty lines
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sh -c "sed -i '/^$/d' core.lst" WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sh -c "sed -i '/^$/d' modules.lst" WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})

# We create a separate list with only dictionary .idl files, they will serve as
# input file list for idl_compiler.py (so we can compile everything in one pass)
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sh -c "find core/ -name *.idl |grep -E 'Init.idl|Bag.idl|Options.idl|Properties.idl|Descriptors.idl|InternalDictionary|CanvasContextCreationAttributes.idl' > ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/dicts_core.lst" WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sh -c "find modules/ -name *.idl |grep -E 'Init.idl|Bag.idl|Options.idl|Parameters.idl|Descriptor.idl|Range.idl|Attributes.idl|Constraints.idl|Data.idl|Filter.idl|Capability.idl|InternalDictionary|MediaTrackConstraintSet.idl|ServicePortConnectResponse.idl|NFCMessage.idl|NFCRecord.idl|FileSystemFlags.idl|NotificationAction.idl|MediaKeySystemConfiguration.idl' |grep -E -v 'VREyeParameters.idl|VRDisplayEventInit.idl|VRFrameData.idl|VRStageParameters.idl|IDBKeyRange.idl|BluetoothAdvertisingData.idl|BluetoothRemoteGATTDescriptor.idl|BluetoothScanFilterInit.idl|RequestDeviceOptions.idl|PushMessageData.idl|PushSubscriptionOptions.idl|PushSubscriptionOptionsInit.idl|MediaSettingsRange.idl' > ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/dicts_modules.lst" WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p bindings/scripts/ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p bindings/core/v8/ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p bindings/modules/v8/ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})

# We create intermediary .pickle files aggregating all the .idl interface names
# Create "core" .pickle files
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python bindings/scripts/compute_interfaces_info_individual.py --cache-directory ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/scripts --idl-files-list ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core.lst --interfaces-info-file ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/core/InterfacesInfoCoreIndividual.pickle --component-info-file ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/core/ComponentInfoCore.pickle WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
# Create "modules" .pickle files
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python bindings/scripts/compute_interfaces_info_individual.py --cache-directory ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/scripts --idl-files-list ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/modules.lst --interfaces-info-file ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/modules/InterfacesInfoModulesIndividual.pickle --component-info-file ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/modules/ComponentInfoModules.pickle WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
# Create an aggregating ("core"+"modules") .pickle file
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python bindings/scripts/compute_interfaces_info_overall.py ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/core/InterfacesInfoCoreIndividual.pickle ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/modules/InterfacesInfoModulesIndividual.pickle ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/modules/InterfacesInfoOverall.pickle WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

# We *really* compile all .idl -> .cpp,.h !
# here, to pass a source file list, we use "--impl-output-dir --generate-impl"
# with "dicts.lst" as a last argument (see its generation above)
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python bindings/scripts/idl_compiler.py --cache-dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/scripts --output-dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/core/v8 --info-dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings --impl-output-dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/core/v8 --generate-impl --target-component core ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/dicts_core.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python bindings/scripts/idl_compiler.py --cache-dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/scripts --output-dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/modules/v8 --info-dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings --impl-output-dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/bindings/modules/v8 --generate-impl --target-component modules ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/dicts_modules.lst WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})


# DEVTOOLS GENERATION

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p resources/inspector/ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND mkdir -p devtools/ WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR})

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python devtools/scripts/build/generate_supported_css.py core/css/CSSProperties.json5 ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/resources/inspector/SupportedCSSProperties.js WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python ${INSPECTOR_DIR}/ConcatenateProtocols.py core/inspector/browser_protocol.json ${V8_DIR}/src/inspector/js_protocol.json ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core/inspector/protocol.json WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python devtools/scripts/build/code_generator_frontend.py ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/core/inspector/protocol.json --output_js_dir ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/resources/inspector WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python devtools/scripts/build/build_release_applications.py inspector toolbox --input_path devtools/front_end --output_path ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/resources/inspector --debug 1 WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})

EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND sh -c "find devtools/front_end -type f -name *.js -o -name *.css -o -name *.json > ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/static.lst" WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
EXECUTE_PROCESS(COMMAND python devtools/scripts/build/generate_devtools_grd.py ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/resources/inspector/InspectorBackendCommands.js ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/resources/inspector/SupportedCSSProperties.js ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/resources/inspector/inspector.html ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/resources/inspector/toolbox.html devtools/front_end/devtools_compatibility.js --static_files_list ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/static.lst --relative_path_dirs devtools/front_end ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/resources/inspector --images devtools/front_end/Images --output ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/devtools/devtools_resources.grd WORKING_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_SOURCE_DIR})
